AtlasLoot:
- Removed the ability to load all modules from the root AtlasLoot directory.  This means that if WoWAceUpdater is not set to unpackage the mod, you need to download all the LoD modules seperately.  The reason for this is that not all updaters people are using support filelist.wau packages and as such were loading everything at startup whether they want to or not.
